\item[{}]{{\bf reader}}

\begin{DoxyCode}
\{                                                                \(\backslash\)
    assert( (\hyperlink{core__c_8h_a7ebac5ed63ddbe66c0f60ac295fc8442}{reader}).\hyperlink{core__c_8h_a9ebd7e76cd02fea0cba96d4c9ce25787}{seq}->elem\_size == \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(\hyperlink{core__c_8h_a3af7387cc1cc7f4c6c88660faa0c3aea}{elem}));            \(\backslash\)
    memcpy(&(\hyperlink{core__c_8h_a3af7387cc1cc7f4c6c88660faa0c3aea}{elem}), (\hyperlink{core__c_8h_a7ebac5ed63ddbe66c0f60ac295fc8442}{reader}).\hyperlink{core__c_8h_a166529da793cc1ef241cff347f3db5a5}{ptr}, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}((\hyperlink{core__c_8h_a3af7387cc1cc7f4c6c88660faa0c3aea}{elem})));               
      \hyperlink{core_2types__c_8h_aa0060cbc242ede391fe041f4f66a681b}{\(\backslash\)}
\hyperlink{core_2types__c_8h_aa0060cbc242ede391fe041f4f66a681b}{    CV\_PREV\_SEQ\_ELEM}( \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(\hyperlink{core__c_8h_a3af7387cc1cc7f4c6c88660faa0c3aea}{elem}), \hyperlink{core__c_8h_a7ebac5ed63ddbe66c0f60ac295fc8442}{reader} )                     \(\backslash\)
\}
\end{DoxyCode}

(   assert(\textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}((\hyperlink{core__c_8h_a9ebd7e76cd02fea0cba96d4c9ce25787}{seq})->\hyperlink{core__c_8h_a1f883233876ef3ed7b1b69454c26c2af}{first}[0]) == \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(\hyperlink{structCvSeqBlock}{CvSeqBlock}) &&      \(\backslash\)

    (\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned})((\hyperlink{core__c_8h_a9ebd7e76cd02fea0cba96d4c9ce25787}{seq})->\hyperlink{core__c_8h_a1f883233876ef3ed7b1b69454c26c2af}{first}->count) ?                            \(\backslash\)
    (\hyperlink{core__c_8h_a9ebd7e76cd02fea0cba96d4c9ce25787}{seq})->\hyperlink{core__c_8h_a1f883233876ef3ed7b1b69454c26c2af}{first}->data + (\hyperlink{core__c_8h_a750b5d744c39a06bfb13e6eb010e35d0}{index}) * \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(elem\_type) :           \(\backslash\)
    cvGetSeqElem( (\hyperlink{structCvSeq}{CvSeq}*)(\hyperlink{core__c_8h_a9ebd7e76cd02fea0cba96d4c9ce25787}{seq}), (\hyperlink{core__c_8h_a750b5d744c39a06bfb13e6eb010e35d0}{index}) )))
